grogdj/Activiti;cc14630f1;Async executor improvement: before, when executing an exclusive job and when not able to get the lock, the executing thread would be stalled for an amount of time and the locking would be retried until the process instance can be locked. This is now changed to not wait+retry, but 'release' the job again (similar to the 'queue full' behavior), thus making the executing thread free again.

grogdj/Activiti;0471c05e2;Added a new async executor setting 'defaultQueueSizeFullWaitTime' setting. This setting will be used when jobs are acquired, but the job queue was full. In this case the job acquisition threads will wait for the amount of time in this setting before doing the query again, giving the queue a bit of a pause. By default set to 0, as to be compatible with the old behaviour.
